15a1(1): 'di ni shAkya'i rigs dga' bar mdzad pa/ thabs cad mkhyen pa/ thams cad gzigs pa yin te/ lam 'di nas tshur shegs kyis bdag gis bsnyen
15a2(1): bkur mi byar mi rung ngo snyam nas yang des bsams pa/ gal te bdag zag 'di las rkang gis babs na ni/ bcom ldan 'das la tha la bar 'gyur gyis zag 'di nas bdag
15a3(1): gis mchongs dang / bdag gis bsnyen bkur byed khom mo snyam du bsams nas/ drag ka de nyid nas mchongs so// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis der sa gzhi shing bal gyi nang tshangs
15a4(1): can 'dra ba byin gyis rlabs nas/ de lhung ma thag tu rkang pas 'greng bar 'gyur te/ dga' bar gyur nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der song nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi
15a5(1): zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ phyi bzhin du 'brang ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de la thugs rje ba'i phyir lam nas gzur te/ phyogs gcig tu bzhugs nas
15a6(1): des kyang bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan sngar 'jug go// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de la de dang mthun pa'i chos
15a7(1): bstan te/ desen brang ze'i khye 'a grel pos san de nyid la 'dug bzhin du 'den pa rtogs pa'i mdo la/ phyir bi 'ong ba'i 'bras bu mngon sum du byas te/ des bden pa mthong nas
15a8(1): san las langs te pra gos mag pa cig tu gzar nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la 'de logs su thal mo sbyang ba btud de/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// 
15b1(1): btsun pa bdag legs par gsungs pa'i chos 'dul ba rab tu byung ba dang / bsnyen par rdzogs shing dge slong gi dngos po thob tu rung na/ bdag kyang bcom ldan 'das
15b2(1): kyi thad du tshangs par spyod pa spyad par 'tshal lo// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong tshur shog ces bya ba'i tshig gis de rab tu byung ste/ bsnyen par rdzogs par
15b3(1): mdzad nas de lung yang pog go// des kyang brtson pa dang / bslab pa dang / bad pas nyon mongs pa thams cad spangs nas/ dgra bcom pa nyid mngon sum du byas
15b4(1): te de dgra bcom pa khams gsum pa'i 'dod chags dang bral bar gyur nas/ gser dang bong par mnyam pa na mkha' dang lag mthil du 'dra ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ 
15b5(1): tsan dan spangs pa lta bur bsil bar gyur pa'i rig pas sgong de'i sbubs bcom pa/ rig pa dang / mngon par shes pa dang / so so yang dag par rig pa thob pa/ 
15b6(1): srid pa'i rnyed pa dang / chags pa dang / bkur sil mi lta ba dang / dbang po dang nyeda'ang dang brgyas pa'i lha rnams kyis mchod cing brjod pa dang / gus par smra ba'i gnas
15b7(1): su gyur to// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de dang pa dang mos pa dang ldan pa rnams kyis mchog tu bstan to// de nas dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa/ 
15b8(1): btsun pa tshe dang ldan pa gel pos bcom ldan 'das mthong nas brag ka nas rang gis mchongs pa dang / gzhan yang 'dis bcom ldan 'das mnyes par bgyis te/ mi mnyes
16a1(1): par ma bgyis la bcom ldan 'das kyi bstan pa la rab tu byung nas nyon mongs pa thams cad spangs te/ dgra bcom pa nyid mngon sum du bgyis pa la gzig
16a2(1): bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ da ltar 'ba' zhig mi yin te/ 'das pa'i dus na yang 'dis ji ltar nga mthong nas/ brag ka nas rang gis 'chongs te nga'i thad du rab tu byung / 
16a3(1): nas bsam gtan bzhi dang / mngon par shes pa lnga bskyed pa de nyon cig/ dge slong dag sngon 'byung ba 'das pa'i dus na drang srong zhig 'khor lnga brgya dang lam du zhugs te/ de brag drung
16a4(1): logs nas 'gro ba las/ phyogs gcig tu 'jug go// thag de'i ngan ni dka' thub can zhig 'jug pa las/ de nas drang song thag drung de na 'jug pa de mthong nas/ mdzang
16a5(1): mthag tu de la shin tu dgang ba skyes te/ des bsams pa/ bdag drang srong de la bsnyen pak+Shar khyod du 'gro'o snyam nas/ des yang bsams pa/ gal te bdug gis rkang
16a6(1): babs na ni drang srong de rdal du 'ong ngo snyam rang gis thag de'i kha nas mchongs pa las/ drang srong des lha la sgo nas lag nas bzung se sa la bzhag go// de nas de'i thad du song ste rkang
16a7(1): pal phyag 'tshal nas/ chos mnyan pa'i phyir mdun du 'jug go// de nas drang song des de la nges par 'byung ba dang / mthun pa'i gtam byas nas/ de de'i thad du rab tu byu
16a8(1): de rab byung nas bsam gtan bzhi dang / mngon par shes pa lnga bskyed do// dge slong dag rje sam du sems/ de'i che chang song ma gyur pa byang chub sems dpa'i sbyod
16b1(1): ba la gnas pa gang yin pa de ni nga yin no// de'i tshe dka' thub can du gyur pa gang yin pa de ni gel kho na yin te/ de'i tshe yang 'dis pa mthong nas brag ka nas rang gis mchongs / 
16b2(1): nga'i thad du rab tu byung nas nas bsam gtan bzhi dang / mngon par shes pa lnga skyed do// da ltar yang nga mthong nas brag ka nas rang gis mchongs te/ nga nyid kyi bstan pa la rab
16b3(1): tu byung nas nyon mongs pa thams cad spangs nas/ dgra bcom pa nyid mngon sum du byas so// de nas dge slong rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la yang zhus pa/ btsun pa ge la
16b4(1): po 'dis las ci bgyis na/ las de'i rnam par smin pa 'dis bcom ldan 'das mnyes par bgyis te/ mi mnyes par ma bgyis la/ bcom ldan 'das kyi bstan pa lar
16b5(1): tu byung nas nyon mongs pa thams cad spangs te/ dgra bcom pa nyid mngon sum du bgyis nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis dad pa dang / mos pa dang ldan pa rnams kyi mchog/ 
16b6(1): tu bstan lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ smon lam gyi dbang las gyur to// gsol pa/ btsun pa 'dis gangang smon lam btab lags/ bka'
16b7(1): stsal pa/ dge slong dag sngon byang ba 'das pa'i dus na bskal pa bzang po 'di nyid la skye gu'i tshe lo nyi khri thub pa na/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhar
16b8(1): su ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs pa/ 'jig rten mkhyen pa skyes bu gdul ba'i kha lo basbyar ba/ bla na med pa la dang mi rnams kyi ston pa/ sangs rgyas bcom
21a1(1): bum ngon sum du byas te/ nges bden pa mthong nas san las langs te/ blagos zag pa gcig tu gzar nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der logs
21a2(1): su bral mo sbyar ba bdud de/ bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// btsun pa bdag legs par gsungs pa'i chos 'dul ba la rab tu byung ba dang / bsnyen par rdzogs shing dge
21a3(1): spong gi dngos po thob tu rung na/ bdag kyang bcom ldan 'das kyi thad du tshangs par spyod pa sbyang bar 'tshal lo// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dge slong tshur shog ces bya ba'i tshig gis rab
21a4(1): byung ste/ bsten par tshogs par mdzad nas/ de la lung yang zag go// des kyang brtson pa dang / bsgrub pa dang / 'bang pas nyon mongs pa thams cad spangs nas/ dgra bcom pa nyid
21a5(1): mngon sa pa byas te/ de dgra bcom pa nyid khams gsum pa'i 'dod chags dang bral bar gyur nas gser ngange bong bar mnyam pan pakha' dang lag mthil du 'dra ba'i sems dang ldan pa/ tsan+dan
21a6(1): spangs la bar bsil bar gyur pa/ rig pas skonga'i spangs bcom pa/ rig pa dang mngon pa shes pa dang / so so yang dag par rig pa thob pa srid pa'i brnyed pa dang / chags pa dang
21a7(1): bkur stsal ma la ba dang / dbang po dang / nye dbang dang bcas pa'i lha rnams kyis mchod cing brjod pa dang / zas par smra ba'i gnas su byung ngo // de nas dge slong rnams kyis/ sangs
21a8(1): rgyas bcom ldan 'das la gsol pa/ btsun pa drang srong 'di 'chibs 'jigs shing bsras nas bcom ldan 'das kyi thang du mchis te/ bcom ldan 'das kyis rab tu byung nas ga
21b1(1): la mang rdzub pa/  pa da drwa pa'i na las 'das bral bdag pa lag gas/ ma ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal ba/ da lar 'dra' thog pa yin te/ ri lta
21b2(1): pa'i rdzas na yang 'di nyid 'tsho bas 'jigs shing srag nas rab tu byung ste/ ngas ma gtan bzhi dang / mngon par shes pa lnga la bkod pa de nyon cig/ dge slong dag sngon 'das pa'i dus na dka'
21b3(1): rngub kyi gnas shig na drang song mngon par shes pa lnga dang ldan pa/ rdzu 'phrul che zhing mthu che ba zhig gnas pa de'i slob ma bram ze'i khye'u le lo can tshe thung ngu zhig yod de/ des de la
21b4(1): yung log kyang de le lo che ba'i phyir bsgrim du mi btub bo// de nas kyi zhig na drang srong des bltas na bram ze'i khye'u de zhag bdun na 'chi bar 'gyur ba mthong na/ des ci yang mthong bar
21b5(1): rig nas/ des skyob sred pa'i phyir smras pa/ bram ze'i khye'u le lo ma byed cig/ khyod ni zhag bdun na 'chi bar 'gyur ro zhes byas so// de nas de thos pathag tu bram ze'i khye'u de shin
21b6(1): tu mi dga' bar gyur te/ mi dga' bar gyur pa des na/ bas pa gtan bzhi dang / mngon par shes pa lnga bskyed do// dge slong dag ci sa mdu sems de'i tshe drang song du gyur pa byang chub
21b7(1): sems dpa'i spyod pa la gnas pa gang yin pa de ni nga nyid yin no// de'i cha bram ze'i rtse'ung byur pa gang yin pa ni drag po 'di khon yin te/ rwa'i tshe yang 'di 'chi bas 'jigs shing
21b8(1): bsrub nas pasam gtan bani dang / mngon par shes pa lnga la gnag go// nga lar yang 'dri shings 'jigs shing bsrag nas rab tu phyung ste/ g.yung drung gi mthar thab pa/ 
23a1(1): sems dpa'i btsun por phu lo// de nas grags 'dzin pa'i rkyen gyis byang chub sems dpa' khye'u mda' thogs dang shin tu mdza' bar gyur to// de nas
23a2(1): gang gi tshe byang chub sems dpas rgan po dang / nang pa dang / shi ba gzigs nas/ nags kyi nang du gnas bcas pa de'i tshe/ khye'u mda' thogs shin tu mi dga' bar
23a3(1): gyur te/ ci zhig mthong na 'khod los bsgyur pa'i rgyal srid dang / bdag gi sring mdor te rab tu byung zhig gras mo// de nas gang gi tshe byang chub sems dpa' blan med pa'i ye shes
23a4(1): bsres nas gdul bar bya ba'i don mdzad cing ser su'i gnas su gshegs te/ yabasas gangan 'jom par mdzad pa ra shAkya stong phrag dum bcom ldan 'das la lta ba dang / bsnyer bkur bya
23a5(1): ba'i phyir ro // shAkya mda' thogs ni sngar mi dga' bar gyur pas/ bcom ldan 'das la ngalta zhing 'gror ma 'dub nas/ de shAH rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi thad du nan gyis khrid nas/ 
23a6(1): gzhon nu bar 'dzugs kyang shAkya rnams kyi sems bsrung ba'i phyir/ bcom ldan 'das las bsrab pa'i gzhi lnga banos so// de nas de lci zhig na de'i sngon mi dga' ba'i phyir blo skyes pa/ bdag gis
23a7(1): mas sa pa'i gni ngas da /  kya bdag kyis de ngasra pa'i bani la khabang cig srung de dgasas su rangs/ des ston pa dgu'ang byur bsla pa'i gni lnga nyams par byas
23a8(1): ma ba 'dran pas kyis chog/ bas pa pa'i bzhin pa mangs 'dal thams brgyags sa pa 'ang 'a la su thus ma drang ba 'ad ni dmes thams pa
23b1(1): sems can dmyal bar 'gro bar 'gyur na mi rung ngo snyam mo// de nas phyi zhig na shAkya mang po rnams bcom ldan 'das ga la 'dred dong ste lpags nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag
23b2(1): 'tshal te/ phyogs gcig tu 'khod do// phyogs gcig tu 'khod nas shAkya rnams kyis bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// btsun pa shAkya mda' thogs kyis ni bslab
23b3(1): pa'i gzhi rnams nyams par bgyis skye mas 'tshal na bcom ldan 'das kyis dgongs te/ ngan song du mi 'chi bar mdzad du gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis shAkya mang po rnams la cang rmi
23b4(1): gsung bar gnang ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis cang mi gsung bas gnang bar shAkya mang po rnams kyis rig nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs pa la mngon par bskyod cing
23b5(1): rjes su yid rang nas/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo bos phyag 'tshal te/ bcom ldan 'das kyi zad nas dong ngo // de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dgongs pa de'i dang
23b6(1): po yongs su smin par bya dgos snyam du dgongs nas/ bcom ldan 'das re shig de la ci yang bka' ma stsal pa las/ tshe'i lhag ma zhag bdun lus par gzigs nas/ der bcom
23b7(1): ldan 'das kyis dge slong rnams la bka' stsal pa/ shAHmda' thogs ni deng nas zhag bdun 'tsho bar 'gyur ro zhes bka' stsal to// de nas sgra de 'ju mar bcing ba bzhin
23b8(1): du grags ma thag tu shAkya mnga' thogs kyis bdag zhag 'dun na 'chi bar lung bstan to// zhes thos nas/ de bcom ldan 'das la ma dad par byar te/ khang bzangs kyi steng na
24a1(1): 'drug cing skyes pa dang / ma 'dres pa'i rol pa'i sbas rtse zhing dga' mgur spyod do// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis dgongs pa/ ngas de la bye nyan thos chen po dag
24a2(1): la 'atang la/ phyis nga nyid 'gro'o snyam du dgongs nas bcom ldan 'das kyis tshe dang ldan pa ma 'gags pa la bka' stsal pa/ ma 'gags pa song la shAkya mda' thogs la som
24a3(1): shig/ de nas tshe dang ldan pa ma 'gags pas btsun pa de ltar 'tshal lo zhes gsol nas phyi bzhin 'brang ba'i dge sbyong dge slong zhig dang / shAkyab de' thogs kyi khyim du song ngo // 
24a4(1): de nas shAkya mnga' jogs kyis dge slong ma 'gags pa bdag gi khyim du 'ongs shes thos so// thos nas kyang phra ru rol dga' ba'i phyir de'i thad du song nas rkang pa la phyag 'tshal te/ 
24a5(1): chos mnyan pa'i phyir ma ga // me dang ldan par 'gugs pas de yongs su srin par 'thung ba'i btum byas nas kya song ngo // de nas kyid nyin mug gnyis pa la bcom ldan
24a6(1): 'das kyis kun dga' 'i btang ngo // zhag gsum pa lan tshe dang ldan pa mo'u 'gal gyi rnga chen po btang ngo // nag bzhi pa la ni tshe dang ldan pa shA ri'i bu btang nas/ tshe dang ldan
24a7(1): bshA 'i bras de la ci nas de bcom ldan 'das la dang pa skye bar 'gyur ba de la khwa'i chos bas nas/ de 'chi bas 'jigs shing skrag par gyur to// de nas dag lnga bral bcom
24a8(1): ldan 'das kyis de'i sems thugs kyis mkhyen nas par 'thogs kyi khyimajug shegs// de nas shAkya ma 'thogs kyis bcom ldan 'das thag ring po zhig nas mthong ngo // 
24b1(1): mthong nas kyang bcom ldan 'das la shin tu dga' bar gyur to// dga' bar gyur nas bcom ldan 'das kyi gdan bshams te bcom ldan 'das la 'di skad ces gsol to// bcod
24b2(1): ldan 'das tshur gshegs/ bcom ldan 'das gshegs pa leg so// bcom ldan 'das gdan bshams pa la bzhugs su gsol/ de nas bcom ldan 'das gdan pa shams
24b3(1): pa la bzhugs nas/ shAkya mda' thogs kyis bcom ldan 'das kyi zhabs la mgo 'os phyag 'tshal te/ chos mnyan pa'i phyir spyan sngar 'dug go// der bcom ldan 'das kyis
24b4(1): shAkya mda' thobs la bka' stsal pa/ mda' thogs 'di ltar 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa 'di ni 'jigs pa rnams kyi nang na phran tshegs tsam du zad do// 'di lta ste/ sems can dmyal
24b5(1): ba dang / dud 'gro dang / yi dgas rnams kyi ngan song gi 'jigs pa 'di ni 'jigs pa rnams kyi nang na 'jigs pa mchog yin no// des gsol pa/ btsun pa sems can
24b6(1): dmyal ba de dag ji lta bu lags/ de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de skyo ba skyed pa'i phyir rdzu 'phrul gyis khrid de/ sems can dmyal ba chen po brgyad bsan nas/ des gsol pa/ 
24b7(1): btsun pa las gang gis skye bar 'gyur lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ srog gcod pa kun tu spen cing sgoms te/ mang du byas pas sems can dmyal
24b8(1): nga rnams su skye bar 'gyur ro// gal te de nas shi 'phos te mi rnams dang skal ba mnyam par 'dir skyes na yang tshe thung bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin du bcom ldan 'das kyis
25a1(1): de la mi dge 'acwan las tsal baHsa pa bas nas/ 'dzas ma thag tu de lhag par yang 'jigs pa skyes te/ bangadag gis bcom ldan 'das la
25a2(1): bslab pa'i gzhi blangs pa las ma bsrungs na bdag sems can dmyal ba dang / dud 'gro dang / yi dgas rnams su skye bar mi 'gyur grang snyam du bsams nas/ des bslab
25a3(1): pa nyams pa de dag bshags nas/ chos mnyan pa'i phyir spyan sngar 'dug go// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis de la de dang mthun pa'i chos bstan te/ des na shAkya mnga'
25a4(1): thogs kyis san de nyid la 'dug bzhin du 'jig tshogs la lta ba'i ri'i rtse mo mngon po nyi shu me shes rdo rjes bcom nas/ rgyun du zhugs pa'i 'bras bu yangan sum du byas

25b2(1): thu ba bkang nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la bder song ste phyin nas/ lha'i me tog rnams kyis gtor te/ chos mnyan pa'i phyir spyan sngar 'jug go// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis

25b4(1): bstod cing rjes su yid rang ste/ bcom ldan 'das la lan gsum bskor ba byas nas de nyid du mi snang bar gyur to// de shi ba'i tshe shAkya rnams the tsom skyes te/ shAkya mda' thogs
25b5(1): kyis bslab pa nyams par byas te/ chang 'thung na de'i 'gro ba ni gang yin/ skye gnas ni gang yin che phyi ma ni gang yin zhig gu/ mal bdag cag gis don 'di bcom ldan 'das
25b6(1): la zhus pa/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bdag cag la ji skad lung bstan pa de bzhin du bzung bar bya'o zhes zer ro// de nas shAkyamang po dag bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der dong

25b8(1): // btsun pa shAkya mnga' thogs kyis bslang pa nyams par bgyis te/ sems 'tshal na/ btsun pa de'i 'gro ba ni gang lags/ sre gnas ni gang lags/ che chi ni
26a1(1): gang lags/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ grogs po dag lhar skyes so// de dag gis gsol pa/ btsun pa shAkya mnga' thogs kyis

26a3(1): ba bshags te/ rgyur tu zhugs pa'i 'bras bu thob nas lhar skyes so// de nas de thos ma thag tu shAkya rnams ya mtshan du byar te/ de dag ya mtshan du gyur nas smras pa/ kye la
26a4(1): sangs rgyas/ rtse mo ches/ kyes dge 'dun/ rtse mchos legs par gsungs pa/ 'di ltar ngan song du 'gro ba'i sems can dag kyang ngan song nas byung ste/ mthongs dang
26a5(1): par byed de zhes zer nas/ lhag par yang sangs rgyas dang / chos dang / dge 'dun la bkur sa byed pa la zhug so// de nas dge slong rnams kyis sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das la
26a6(1): gsol pa/ btsun pa shAkya mda' thogs 'chi bas 'jigs shing skrag pa las/ bcom ldan 'das kyis 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa las skyabs mdzad de/ g.yung drung gi mthar thug
26a7(1): bgrub pa dang / bde ba'i mya ngan las 'das pa la bzhag pa la gzigs/ bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/ da ltar 'ba' zhig ma yin te/ ji ltar 'das pa'i dus na/ 
26a8(1): yang 'di 'chibs 'jigs shing bsra ga nas zhag bdun bsa'apa bsungs te/ gni ri las mthangs sa sres par can cig/ dge slong dag sngon 'byung ba 'das pa'i du
26b1(1): bsal ba bzang po 'di nyid la skye gu'i tshe lo nyi khri thub pa na/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rig pa dang zhabs su ldan pa/ bde bar gshegs pa 'jig rten mkhyen pa/ 
26b2(1): skyes bu gdul ba'i kha lo bsgyur ba/ bla na med pa/ lba dang mi rnams kyi ston pa sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das 'od srung zhes bya ba 'jig rten du byung ste/ de'i tshe grong khyer lnga
26b3(1): ra nA sir tshong pa dbul po zhig 'jug pa des/ phyi zhig na yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'od srung gi bstan pa la dad pa rnyed do// tshong pa de yang sbyin pa la sred pa zhig
